Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout .i. spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme: puis met ou pertus .i. clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi .iij. jors ou iiij. et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	Sometimes children are born without an opening in the penis, or with a small opening, or it is not in its place. In this case, he must immediately pierce it with a very thin spatulum according to this shape: then put into the opening a very thin piece of lead, and tie it and hold it there for three or four days; and when he wants to urinate, remove the plug and let him urinate, and then replace it. And perhaps it is not necessary, because the urine that comes out will not let it close.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera. Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut; et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	Those whose opening is small, if they are treated with the lead plug as we have said, will be enlarged. Those who do not have the opening in its proper place are troubled, for some are born with the opening at the tip of the penis, and because of this they cannot urinate without lifting their penis upward; and they cannot ejaculate because the matter cannot reach the glans, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the way to treat it is for the patient to lie on his back, then the head and glans of the penis are raised up like a feather, as thick as a pen, so that the opening is in the middle, as it should be; and beware of bleeding which often occurs there, and if it does, stanch the flow with something that stops blood, and cure the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of pustules on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many times this albata occurs on the penis, and it is an ugly-looking growth; there are both malignant and non-malignant types; therefore you must take them with a small, sharp knife, cut them and clean them all, then put wet cotton in Egyptian ointment on top; then cure with thin ointment until they are healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere. Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer. Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the albata is malignant, of a pus color and foul-smelling, then you must apply cautery. When you have cut it, and if the albata is in the head of the penis, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, then you must first remove the albata that is inside; and when it is healed, cure the outside. For if you cure them together, the penis will not be secure from being pierced, and blackness and corruption will come in its head and testicles; so cut away all that is black and rotten, then apply ointment of honey and flour made from pomegranate bark and rosebuds, then cure with other cures until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme: Li cauteres si aide as .ij. dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a .i. estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And if the albata is in the penis and cannot be removed from the skin, then cut it and cure with ointment of wax and pomegranate bark and rosebuds and flour, and anoint the albata with honey; then apply cautery, and it will be healed.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a .i. spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre .ij., et i met .i. subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	and if it is difficult to treat this, you should cut into it with a spatumile at the tip of the penis and scrotum; then gently pull apart, and place a fine wet linen cloth in cold water, so that it does not dry out again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not a matter of continence like other wounds; nevertheless, when we perform this act of our own will, and properly on infants, it is necessary that we make the best and lightest cut for their salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not mention the circumcision of their infants, for they did not practice it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For I have seen most of the masters and surgeons who perform circumcision all around the foreskin, some forcefully, and on all new borns; thus, the head of the penis would become inflamed as there are two membranes, and by chance one gets pushed upwards while the other remains underneath.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Then they cover it again, and the pain becomes doubled, and at the purification which is done on the foreskin isn't secured the tip of the member; and at the purification of the nail sometimes the cautery slips and ruins the work, and many times they are born such that they don't need purification, and I have seen this.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the purification that is done forcefully all around the thread of hair, I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut justly both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en .i. tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	For when you press your hand, you cut evenly all around the thread; but let the thread be well wrapped around the skin; and let the manner of the first operation be such that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around the penis, and then let him move it in every way he can.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz .i. poc a .i. autre liien; et la tien as .ij. dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les .ij. liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	then have him stand upright between your hands, and hide the strength in your hands or under your feet so that the infant does not see it, nor any of the instruments; then put your hand on the penis and breathe or blow on the heart, and pull it up until the head of the penis is inside; then cleanse it well of the dirt that has accumulated there, then tie the place marked with a double thread, then tie it underneath from .i. to another string; and hold it at .ij. for the second time at the pouch and at the index finger, and press between the .ij. strings, then lift the heart quickly and pull the head of the penis;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre .i. drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then let the blood flow a little at a time, for that is the muedres; and put powder on top of the powder 1. a piece of cloth glued with a half-cooked egg yolk tempered with rose water, cooked with good and fresh rose oil, and let it stay until the next day, and treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The shape of the forces for purification is as follows: both heads should be tense and pointed, and the heads should be as large as the palm equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	the error of purification is when the pus within the incision has dried up; therefore, you must extend it with your nail, so that the pus forms an abscess; and then cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your nail, hold it with tweezers and then cut.
Et s’il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if it persists for 3 days, and that which is beneath the foreskin is swollen, let it be until the abscesses are healed and the skin slightly peeled; then cut it as much as you can, and beware of the foreskin, it will not harm him in any way.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore, heal the area of the wound with powder, as we have said in the treatise on powders; and if it cuts too deeply into the skin, and it goes above, it will not harm him; therefore, heal it, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to a stone, or frozen blood, or a growth, or similar things that we have mentioned in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie, et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And if the urine is not released and you see that it is retained due to a stone that is lodged in the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent over at the knees, with his feet placed on his back, and he should stretch his abdomen from above his back, and restrain himself as much as he can; this will force the neck of the bladder upwards, causing the expression of the stone and the release of urine.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	And if it does not come out as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you should use a device called a 'syringe', of which this is the form: it should be made of thin silver, light as an owl's feather; the tube should be a palm and a half in length, with a thin nozzle at the end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren .i. fil double, et lie au chief .i. poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And the way to make the urine pass is that you take a double thread, and tie to the end of it a little ball of wool or cotton, and insert the end of the thread into the syringe; and squeeze out the excess wool and push it up to the end of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or lard and egg white, and make the patient sit on a chair, and anoint his bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	then gently insert the syringe into the penis so that it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis downward toward the scrotum; then fill the syringe up to the bladder, and you will feel the patient's urine flow into the empty vessel, but if this is not done according to this order, because the conductor where it goes is twisted, then pull out the thread all the way through the wool, and the urine will follow the wool, then withdraw it outward, and make the urine flow;
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and use the syringe again until the bladder is emptied, and be careful of the patient.
des maladies de la vessie	of diseases of the bladder:
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When burns or blood come in the bladder, or pus is accumulated there, and you see water and medicine distilling, then do this to all of the instrument that is called "clepsydra", and it is formed:
Elle est close, et si a .iij. pertus: .ij. d’une part, et .i. d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	It is closed and has 3 openings: 2 on one side and 1 on the other, as you can see; and the end through which the medicine flows should be such that it blocks the tube well without any addition, so that one may draw out moisture and push it in when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	and when you see your medicines flowing into the bladder, place the end of the catheter in the moisture and draw it out through the tube that is there; then push the tube firmly in again; then the moisture will enter the catheter and go into the bladder immediately, so that the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	and this is the form of the subtle enema by which one enemas the bladder: it is made like this:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a .i. sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les .ij. seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe .i. poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	And it is made of silver or brass, and the head is higher up; and below there is .i. breast or the .ij. breasts meet; then take a lamb's bladder and put in the moisture which you see is clotting the bladder, then tie it between the .ij. breasts with a double thread, and heat .i. pot of this moisture over the fire; then pour the head of the catheter into the penis, then hold your hand over the bladder until all the moisture has gone in comfortably, so that the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai .i. cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute .i. fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble .i. dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, and make 1 circle out of it, and pierce it all around; then thread a strong string through these holes, then assemble the circle as one assembles a dal, and put inside what you see of oil and moisture and water, and tie it in the instrument; and do as you did with the bladder, by pressing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division the methods of stone extraction, along with medicines; and I have said the difference between a stone lodged in the urethra, and all the signs, and in which type of stone one should operate on cutting; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that the urine exits from the bladder resembling water in its subtlety; and it opens up like an onion, and the patient feels pain in his penis, and he can urinate many times, and then it blocks again; and many of these stones cause a fundament; and the healing is easier for children until they are four years old, and it is very serious in the elderly, and it is intermediate in those who are between youth and old age; and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines. Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	And when we come to the cure, it is appropriate first to cleanse the patient with an enema, in order to draw out all the feces which are in the intestines. For they sometimes obstruct the retrieval of the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche ded ens;	Then take the patient by the feet and lift him up and move him around, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from the top; then let him sit between your hands which are prepared, and his hands are under his thighs, so that his bladder is completely tilted downward; then you probe and touch it inside.
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere. Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	If you feel the stone in the space, then hurry to cut it with a knife. And if it does not come out with touching alone, then wet your index finger of the left hand with oil, if the patient is an adult, or with your middle finger, if the patient is an adolescent; and insert it into his anus, and probe for the stone, and when you feel it on your finger, push it towards the neck of the bladder; then press with your finger, and cut where you feel the need to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the minister to press the bladder with his hand, and tell him to extend his fingers up with his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin under the testicles in the area where one performs the incision; then he fills the spatulum, which is the mold.
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And cut between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but along the left side of the navel; and it should be straight over the stone, and both testicles should be pressed against the anus, and the incision should be diagonal so that it is wide at the top and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	Perhaps it will press the testicle that is against the anus so that it pops out without effort; and you should know that there is stone which has angles and edges: one type grinds its way out; and there is another which is under, similar to a grape, and round, whose exit is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li .i. estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge .i. poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	For that one with angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not pop out, then you must pull it out with tweezers which are like a file at the tip, to pull out the stone so that it doesn't slip away; or you fill under it a very thin instrument, and if you cannot catch it that way, then widen the opening a little, and if the blood is exposed, then stop it with vitriole;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors. Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie. Car .ij. choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	if there is more than one stone, then plug the largest first into the neck of the bladder, then press upwards, then draw it out, and the smaller ones afterwards if there are several. And if it is very large, then it must be cut, and a larger wound made. For two things happen to the patient: either he dies, or the urine comes out where the urethra cannot heal; but nevertheless, try to draw it out, or break it up with forceps, until you have drawn it out in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus .i. drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	and when you have finished your work, apply the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and hold it, and put on top a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess; then re-bandage the patient over his neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the area well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	And if hot abscesses and blood clots come in the wound and congestion of blood in the bladder, and it is retained so that the urine does not pass out easily with the urine: then press your finger into the wound, and extract that blood, for if any remains, it will corrupt the bladder and burst.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les .ij. cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	Then raise the wound with salt and vinegar and oil, and help it in every way you know how until it is healed; and whenever you treat it during the day, tie the two thighs together and apply the medicine to the affected area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure. Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	And if the stone is small and lodged in the urethra, causing urination to be blocked; then the treatment I described above is sufficient, even if you have to cut him many times, as I have experienced myself.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take an iron needle with three pointed ends and insert it into a hot brand:
puis pren .i. fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge. Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	then take a thread and tie it around the urethra below the stone so that it cannot go back into the bladder; then push the needle into the urethra gently until it reaches the stone; and turn the needle in the stone with your hand little by little, until you pierce the stone from another side; then the urine will come out at once, press your hand on what is left of the stone inside the urethra. As soon as it breaks, it will come out with the urine and the patient is healed;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie .i. fil desoz la piere et .i. autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les .ij. liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cannot do this for any reason that defies it, tie a thread under the stone and another one above it, then make the wand straight on the stone between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the thread, and cleanse the congealed blood in the wound; and cure it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone is lodged in women's bodies, and if it does, the cure is difficult due to three reasons: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; the second is that one cannot find a skilled female healer who can be trusted, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.	The third reason is that one cannot find a skilled female healer in the art of medicine; and the fourth is that women's stones are often deeper than men's, so a deeper incision is required, and there is great fear involved.Et il est grant diference entre li piere des homes et de la femme: car li piere de l’ome si est en leu plus fenestrez et plus pluzible a trover et a tailler, et la piere de la femme si est plus parfont et plus emmiée.
Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier .i. caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And if you need to go to the toilet, then you should take a small amount of well-prepared dung and apply it, and if you cannot find any, then use a small amount of fine earth; and show him a wise old woman who is experienced in matters relating to women, or a woman who knows something about medicine, and instruct her to do what you tell her regarding the examination of the stone.
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And be sure to check if the woman is a virgin: then she should press her finger into her vagina and look for the stone; and if she finds it, she should push it out with her finger, and you must instruct her to press her left hand firmly against her bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	If she finds it, then she should move the stone gradually from the entrance of the bladder all the way down to the root of the thigh; then press on the stone at the root of the thigh towards the middle of the groin, where it is most sensitive; and feel for the stone in that area. She should not move her finger above or below the stone, and the incision should be made small at first;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains. si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	then insert the thread into the incision, if you feel that the stone is sharp and cut the flesh so that the stone can come out; and know that there are many types of stones: small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and those with horns. Know their likenesses in order to understand how they will come out.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	And if the blood flows, put in its place powdered vitriol and hold it for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your work, so that the stone comes out, and have the instruments that I told you about for extracting stones to help you with your task.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood flows and it is from an artery that has been cut, put powder on the wound and press it with bandages and bindings, and do not release it again, and leave the stone and do not pull it out, as the patient might die; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, return to your work so that the stone comes out.
de hernie carnouse	of meat hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Ramice aquouse is nothing other than an accumulation of moisture or white pus, which is located under the heart of the testicles, within the egg; and it is called "pus," and sometimes it is properly located in the membrane of the egg, if one believes that it is not the same egg.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ramice is due to weakness that comes to the testicles and is spread out from there.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colours; it may be a yellow colour, or red, or black, or a watery white, and more besides.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, .i. poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to recognize this accumulation; if it is in the white pus that we have mentioned, then it is a reon, like an egg, small and round like an egg, and does not burst the testicle, for it has moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the fabric itself, then the abscesses will be filled with part of the yolk, and because of this people think it's another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white part of the scrotum, then it feels good; therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, you should test all the way around, from which the form is as follows.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then, what comes after the insertion point, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	And when we cure it with iron, then the patient should be bled according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he should lie on his back, on something a little high, and put a lot of cushions under him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des .ij. costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on his left side and instruct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the wand to one of the two ribs of the heart;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the lead spatula and cut the skin of the testicles through their length up to the scrotum, and make the incision straight while describing the skin of the testicles until you reach the white subcutaneous tissue, and carefully peel it back according to your ability;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	then pierce the subcutaneous tissue with a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then put in your fingers, and stretch out the scrotum upwards; do not touch the testicles themselves, but only the scrotum; cut it all or in pieces just as carefully, for if you do not cut it well, the water will return;
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the scrotum has become detached from your work, then return it to its place when you have finished working on the subcutaneous tissue; then sew up the two lips of the testicles with a single stitch, and then treat the wound as you would any other, until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, then you must tie off the suspended vessels, fearing the flow of blood; then cut open the scrotum throughout its suspension, extract the egg, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en .ij. parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont .ij. ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	And if pus has collected in two parts together, know that these are two pockets; then cut open the other part just as you did the first equally, then wash out the blood and put soft lamb's wool soaked in rose oil into the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les .ij. coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And put another piece of lamb's wool soaked in wine and oil on top, and place it over both testicles, and bind it tightly with a double cloth all around according to this shape:
Puis pren .ij. drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les .ij. angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	Then take two pieces of cloth, and fill them with wool according to this shape, and sew them together at the opening of the pants, and have one piece hold the testicle up against the anus and back, and the other at the part of the groin, and both ends on top of the two thighs; and have all the binding in the loop of the pants.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes .i. cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this ramica of cautery is medicated in the place of an iron brand, and it is that you grip a subtle scalpel, and cut through the skin of the testicles, and it is heated as we have said, so that the white pimple containing pus is revealed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	If one takes the cautery according to this form and pierces the pimple gently, and burns it with this subtle hot cautery;
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	And cut it in all ways that you can, until you have removed everything; and be careful that the fire does not touch the testicle; and know that this action is much safer; and watch out for blood flow and damage from cutting;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything contradicts you, such as a hot abscess or blood flow or anything else, then treat what contradicts you according to what has already been said.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai,	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this procedure because of its horror, then administer a perforation as I have told you, and when you are quite certain by the signs that we have mentioned that the watery fluid is gone,
si fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege leveit; puis perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	then let the patient sit on a high seat; then pierce the abscess in the lower part to the full depth of the spear-head, and insert the perforation into the body; make the holes wide so that all the water flows out;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then put cotton on the spot, and bind it, and let the rest of the water flow out, then treat the wound until it is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge .i. poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés .vj. mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and if the white membrane does not let the water flow out of the wound, then you must insert a pipe or instrument used to treat dropsy, of which the structure is described earlier; enlarge the wound a little, and know that the water will return, and be gathered again after six months or so, and when it is gathered as before, the patient will pass his days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the dissection of this branch there are many dispositions of fear, because of which it seems better to me that one should leave it untouched.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you the work and appearances of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I say therefore that many abscesses come in the body, especially in the testicles; and it is because of various causes.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is to be known by excess of bitterness and bile, which is spread throughout the body, or from a blow.
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body; and it does not subside in pain, and is a serious abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes there is a gray abscess, full of pus and blood, which comes from a vein or a swollen vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from a vein, it is recognized by the hot disposition of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and you must not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois,	Those who are made of wine lees are recognized by their appearance through the touch of the fingers,
et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	and anyone can well judge the quality based on this appearance and other similar characteristics;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and you should cut the skin of the eggs, then the yolks will be on top, and the white part will be beneath, and release the suspension from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already cracked with these new shells, then you must break the egg and crack the shell.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is airy in the face or in those who are inside the vessels, then you must deliver all that membrane and crack it smoothly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the crack is at the back of the shell, then you must crack it all and extract the egg as we have said.Et s’il y a u neuue char ou dedens la tenve, si covient que tu la cope et la delivre, et mets l’uef en autre vaissel.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is done, then dress the wound with soft wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it heals.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a .i. borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions,	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to a plum, with the softening of the testicles,
et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	and the patient groans painfully when he walks;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant,	and the treatment of this disease is also painful like this one before.
et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And yet we will tell you how to treat it according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois,	You should make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then tie the suspensory of testicles tightly with your fingers,
a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	holding all the vessels that are close to the penis, and pulling them upwards, and stretching them firmly;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert,	then cut with a scalpel across the width of the vessels, as far as they are exposed
et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	and then scrape from each side, just as we have said in the extraction of the arteries that are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then he inserts a needle where there is .a. double thread, and ties it at the first place where the vein came from, and ties it directly to the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	then he cuts them in the middle correctly, according to the length of the body, and draws out the corrupted moisture;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	then cure the wound as with the others or wrap it tightly, so that no blood vessels rupture and bleed out from either side.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	this does no harm, and if all the vessels are closed, then one should draw out the clotted blood from all the vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the vein does not lose its clotting because of the incision of the vessels, and they dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rotgut wound
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The causes of this disease are the incisions that come from syphilis, or the swelling on the abdomen in the region of the intestines, causing them to descend from that opening to one of the testicles.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces .ij. manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	and this opening is from syphilis, or from the swelling of it; and these two types of fester come from many causes: from a blow, or a fall, or from straining, or from lifting a heavy load, and from similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs that it is from a syphilitic ulcer are that it occurs bit by bit over a long period of time, and does not come suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are even throughout, up to the depth, because the syphilis presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is of the section of the sinus, that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and there are different abscesses appearing underneath the skin close to the surface, and it is due to the discharge of the intestines and the body from the sinus.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the fester comes with the intestines, and is retained inside, and causes great suffering to the patient, especially when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments using iron, there is fear, which is why one should avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of the treatment is that you command the patient to draw in his intestines with his hand inside the wound if he can reach it;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then press on his neck between your hands, and lift the buttocks
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then turn him over on his back and brush all the hair from his chest
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then push inside the lips of the wound with a hook according to what you need in order to open the wound, and let such that the pus can come out
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then scrape off the scrotum skin that is under the chest skin, until the white, tough scrotum skin is uncovered all over
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac,	then put your index finger in that which follows the anus, in that which is between the white membrane which is under the shell of the egg, and between the second membrane
et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and separate that which is behind the egg, and between the second membrane; and then move the right hand inside the anus, and hold the white membrane up in your left hand, and lift the egg out of all the membranes towards the tail;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the assistant to hold the egg upright, and untie that which is behind the diaper;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and feel with your fingers if there is any intestine wrapped up in or a hard white membrane, and if you find anything, then put it back into the belly underneath;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait .i. gros fil fait de .x. filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait .iiij. filz;	then take a needle with .i. thick thread made of .x. threads, and insert it into the rear part of the scrotum, which is after the skin of the testicles; after the scrotum, then tie the threads that appear, so that there are .iiij. threads;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de .ij. pars;	then tie them one on top of the other in a cross shape, and tie the scrotum, of which we have said is underneath the skin of the testicles, with a strong string of  .ij. parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de .ij. pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the threads around the scrotum and tie them tightly, so that no blood vessels that nourish it can enter, so that an abscess does not form;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc .ij. dois de celui, et aprés ces .ij. liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place the thread according to the first long line of   .ij. parts from that one, and after these   .ij. lines leave the scrotum which is under the skin of the testicles the size of a bean;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	and then the other according to the roundness that the egg carries; then cut into the part which is under the skin of the testicles, as much as the blood flows, and the bowels, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply wool moistened in oil, and place it on the wounds, and then apply the ligature that we have described.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have described is cauterized after the incision, due to doubt about blood flow.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	For this happens many times, and leaves the ligature until it bleeds through; and if it is slow to bleed, then use hot water, and apply what we have said until it bleeds.Car li sans ne peut corer s’i n’est de l’aigue chaude ou feu que nos avons dit.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done like the branch that is together with the vein, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after cutting above gently from below;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then press upon me, and open the abscess of him who works, until the vessels burst; and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	Sometimes the anus tears, as we have said, and the wound opens; and none of the intestines come out, and if they do, it is only a little, and they heal up again in no time.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	But if he stays too long at this point, the wound will fester and the intestines will come out.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	And this happens because of the swelling of the abscess near the anus, as we have said, for it is swollen, then softened and swollen, and the wound opens.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before; and sometimes it is treated with iron in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de .iij. dois;	and the patient lies on his back between your hands, then press the site of the fracture hard with a broad instrument according to the quantity of 3 eggs;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	then pull out the sac which is under the skin where the abscess is, then take the thread and place it on the exposed area of the abscess;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les .ij. leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	then press it deeply into the abdomen, then sew up the 2 exposed areas of the abscess on the head of the thread, and sew one and then the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then pull out the head of the vein, and cover it with nothing but syrup or extend the wound with anything else, as I have made you aware in the treatment of intestinal wounds;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies. Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	then treat it like any other wound. And when you cover the stitches, clean and treat the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	Syrup is constricting and has no appearance in the wound, and cautery is better for this purpose and closer to safety.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men, because the parts inside are softened, and it appears milky white; and when one wishes to treat this, he should make the patient lie on his back, and cut the softened skin on top of the natural skin; then bring together the two edges of the wound with a single stitch, and if you see that there is excess softened skin, sew it shut with three or four stitches firmly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it as you would other wounds until it heals, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	of chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes. Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc .ij. manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.  En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.  Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a .i. cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Do you know that chastisements are forbidden in our law, and because of this I would prefer not to discuss them in this book; and it is only necessary for two reasons: one is so that the surgeon can respond when asked, and understand how to treat them; and the other is because we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as bulls, rams, and horses and other beasts. I say therefore that castration is done in two ways: either by attraction or by cutting. For the method we do by attraction, we make the animal sit in warm water until his testicles are softened and hanging; then grab them with your hand until they are removed and you no longer feel anything. For the castration by cutting: one must tether the animal, and cut the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie off the scrotum, and cut each sac in one place when you have well-scratched them; and I leave some pus and the thin membrane that covers the vessels; and this method of castration is better than the one by attraction, because in the one by attraction sometimes something remains in the testicles, causing the animal to desire lust; then treat the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc .ij. manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les .ij. coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.  Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et .ij. coions.  Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	There are two kinds of hermaphrodites: the first is when between the two genitals there is an opening like a woman's vagina, with pubic hair and sometimes urination occurs from it.  The second type is in women, who have a penis on their groin and two genitals.  The treatment for both men and women is to bandage everything tightly, and treat them as you would other wounds; but for the second type of man, where urine escapes through the skin around the genitals, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure. Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee». Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Tentigene is a swelling on the natural part, so ugly to look at; and some women have it as large as a hand, and that is the cure. You should dye the excess of the testicle with your hand or fingernail, and bandage it lightly; and do not go too deep, so that no bleeding occurs, then cure it with another cure until it is healed; and for one which emerges at the mouth of the womb, use it, and perhaps it will work, and it is according to the likeness of a cow, and therefore they call it the "cow disease". You should bandage it, just as we have said for the testicle, and cure it until it is healed.
de erratique	of erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile. Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait. S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as .ij. leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes .ij. dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les .ij. leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder. Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte. Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez. Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	Erratique is when the nature of the woman is not understood, or the opening is small; and it is by nature from birth, or by accident through illness that has come to be; or it is due to a foreign object, or a sottish tumor, and is formed in the womb, or on the sides, or underneath, or wherever; and it should be understood by examination of the belly. If the tumor is clearly apparent, then you should examine it with your fingers or with a stick. If it is a sottish tumor and it is close to the skin, then you should do this: place the woman on her back with her legs spread out, and form the two lips so that the sottish tumor becomes visible and the tumor is exposed; then take wool, moisten it in oil, and place it over the area, and have the woman lie down for a day or so that it may not adhere. And if the tumor is hard and solid, then you should cut it with a spatulum similar to a bay leaf. If the tumor is made of flesh, then one must suspend it and cut it; and one should use medicines to stop bleeding, such as acacia, dragon's blood, incense, and egg white beaten together; then prepare a broad lance so that the wound may not close up; and this should be for a long time, and one should apply a tent of dry linen; then treat with other treatments until it is healed. And when in the womb there is flesh that has formed, then one must cover it according to this manner, if it is not an abscess. For in an abscess that is in the womb, one should not touch it in order to pierce it.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation. Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer. Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer. Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai .i. emplaustre sus son dos. Et se il estainche, c’est boin. Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.  Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a .i. chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Hemorrhoids are opened veins that bleed without cause, and when hemorrhoids are old, they become throbbers; and we have already described their appearances, signs, and how to treat them. I say that hemorrhoids and throbbers, when they are completely inside the anus and do not appear to the touch, cannot be cured by iron. Those that are at the mouth of the anus can be felt, and they can be treated. Therefore, you should first put the woman in a cold room; then, cut off the hemorrhoids with tongs, and burn their roots; then powder them with medicines that constrict blood vessels, such as acacia and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things; then bind her feet to the wall for an hour, then place her in cold water. If there is any bleeding, let her sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate bark, galls, and similar things; then take barley flour, mix it with honey and garlic, and make a poultice out of it to apply to her back. And if it stops, that's good. If not, make her breathe leeches on her back and breasts without using iron; then take wool, moisten it in plantain juice or dogwood juice mixed with old wine, and make her breathe it in at the affected spot. And when the abscess has subsided, treat the area with ointment until it is healed; and that which is called "albathir" is red and looks like a rough head, so it should be covered as I have said for throbbers; then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	Here is the translation of the text into English:
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division. Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.  Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege, et ait .ij. petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument. Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés .ij. jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.  Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	There are many types of abscesses that occur in the anus, such as ulcers, piercings, herpes, fistulas, hemorrhoids, and hot abscesses, as well as other diseases that I have described in the previous section. Therefore, I will now describe the treatment for a hot abscess that occurs in the anus, which is not among the types that heal quickly. If you want to know how to treat it with iron instruments, observe whether the abscess is soft at the beginning of its appearance, and if it is accompanied by heat and fever, and if it turns red when you look at it. Then, do not rush to pierce it; instead, let the pain subside first. Then, make the patient sit on a low stool or chair, with their feet elevated so that their back is tilted slightly forward, and their knees bent with their arms placed under their knees. Tie their arms securely with a strong cord, then suck the anus to open it and insert the instrument used for this purpose. Check the depth of the anus so that the instrument does not go in too far and injure the patient. If the instrument is large, cover the entrance of the anus with cloth to prevent discomfort. Then, insert the tip of the instrument and apply pressure. When the abscess breaks open and the content is discharged, treat the wound with soft tents dipped in rose oil or virgin oil. Place the tent inside the wound, reaching deep into the anus, and put a pad soaked in warm water or a decoction of mallows on top of the wound and around it. After two days of treatment with suitable ointments, the wound will begin to heal. Sometimes, raising the anus and applying a poultice made of water and honey, followed by a poultice of mallows that have been cooked in water, is beneficial. Then, return to treating the wound with ointments. If the wound has subsided but is still open, refrain from using iron instruments for treatment. Instead, follow the methods described earlier in the text.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
